                                  pcBackupEnabled ? "translate-x-5" : "translate-x-0"
                                }`} />
                              </button>
                            </div>

                            <Button onClick={setupPcBackup} size="sm" className="bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white shrink-0">
                              Setup PC Folder
                            </Button>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        {pcBackupHandle && (
                          <div className="text-[10px] font-medium text-emerald-600/70 bg-emerald-100/50 px-2 py-1.5 rounded border border-emerald-200/50 flex justify-between items-center">
                            <span>✓ Linked to local folder: <b>{pcBackupHandle.name}</b></span>
                            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-4 text-[10px] px-1 text-emerald-700" onClick={() => {
                              setPcBackupHandle(null);
                              setPcBackupEnabled(false);
                              localStorage.removeItem("rupee_ledger_pc_backup_enabled");
                            }}>Disconnect</Button>
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>                          {pcBackupHandle ? (
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={() => syncToPcBackup(pcBackupHandle)} className="border-emerald-200 text-emerald-700 hover:bg-emerald-100">
                                Sync Now
                              </Button>
                              <button
                                type="button"
                                onClick={() => {

                              Setup PC Folder
                            </Button>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        {pcBackupHandle && (
